[32m+[m[32m    <h3>WHAT APITO DOES</h3>[m
[32m+[m[32m    <p>Apito is an online platform that allows users to upload pictures, videos and descriptions which we will then store in a time capsule for several years. The intention is to dig up these time capsules after a predetermined amount of time and reveal all media content and corresponding descriptions for the public to see. Thus, the future generation can see what people were like and what life was like back in previous years.</p>[m
[32m+[m[32m    <p>Users can also use the service to purchase eGifts which can be sent to their family and friends directly through email. An eGift is a virtual gift card that can be used to make purchases on the Apito website.</p>[m
[32m+[m[32m    <p>Finally, we also take donations for those that would like to support our cause and help us fund our project. Donations will primarily be used to provide others with eGifts for use on the Apito website in order to get as many people involved as possible. Donations will also be used to cover some of the project costs.</p><br>[m
[32m+[m[32m    <h3>ACCEPTABLE USE OF THE WEBSITE</h3>[m
